###  Uuno‚ÇÅ

This rare proper noun overlaps more common *Uuno* (FIXME)
* UPOS:  PROPN
* in KOTUS dictionary under:  1
* Origin:  finer|joukahainen|enwikt
* Possible NER class:  FIRST
* Blacklisted:  PROPN-BLOCKING
* Semantic tags:  MALE
